'author_association': 'MEMBER', 'body': 'Some memos:\r\n\r\n+ Found that at present echarts only uses `__extends` function of tslib. (by searching `from "tslib` in echarts/lib.).\r\n+ About bundle size: After tree shaking (tested in vite@6.0.0-beta.9, `tsc -b && vite build`), only used functions of tslib will be included in bundle. That is only `__extends` (and `extendStatics`, which is called by `__extends` internally) is included. So the bundle size is probably not a concern till now.\r\n+ Compatibility if changing to `"tslib": "^x.x.x"`: Checked the commit log of `__extends` on git, there\'s no breaking. Thus this change does not break echarts. \r\n+ Use different versions of tslib in one JS context: (tested in vite@6.0.0-beta.9, `tsc -b && vite build`) , the built bundle is like this :\r\n    ```js\r\n    // At the top scope of the bundle file dist/assets/index-JsGP8STl.js\r\n    // Two tslib are included but the name are modified to avoid conflict.\r\n    var extendStatics$1 = function(d, b) { /* ... */ };\r\n    function __extends$1(d, b) { /* ... */ }\r\n    /* ... */\r\n    var extendStatics = function(d, b) { /* ... */ };\r\n    function __extends(d, b) { /* ... */ }\r\n    ```\r\n', 'reactions': {'url': 'https://api.github.com/repos/apache/echarts/issues/comments/2472880033/reactions', 'total_count': 0, '+1': 0, '-1': 0, 'laugh': 0, 'hooray': 0, 'confused': 0, 'heart': 0, 'rocket': 0, 'eyes': 0}, 'performed_via_github_app': None}]
